How to Roll

Roll a d10 and a d100, minus 1 from the d10.

The d10 is the 100s place and the d100 is the tens and ones.

E.g. if you roll a 10 (-1) and a 56 that's 396.

If you roll a 1 (-1) and a 04 that's 4.

1 (-1) and a 00 becomes 1000.

Loot Chart

#1

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Uncommon
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Red
- Passive: Flying
    - You may now use up to all your Movement Speed to fly each turn. You cannot hover.
- Essence Value: 1000
- Credit Value: 100
- Aesthetic: Valdan (Cyberpunk)

#2

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Uncommon
- Gear Type: Kernel
- Color: Gray
- Passive: Cover Master
    - Bypass half cover; full cover becomes half cover.
    - Your half cover becomes full cover.
- Essence Value: 1000
- Credit Value: 100
- Aesthetic: Valdan (Cyberpunk)

#3

- Gear: Kernel
- Rarity: Uncommon
- Gear Type: Kernel

- Credit Value: 100
